Then I booked this hotel for two nights from Ctrip. We booked three rooms and checked in on May 2. First of all, the check-in was very slow. The front desk staff was a man with average service attitude. The situation of the room after moving in was that the room had a stuffy smell as soon as you entered the door. You must turn on the central air-conditioning for ventilation, but the central air-conditioning cannot adjust the temperature. The elderly feel cold when sleeping at night, and it is very stuffy when it is turned off. It is estimated that the hotel has unified control to save money. In terms of hygiene, you can see that the alarm clock on the bedside table is covered with a layer of dust-like things. It feels very bad and it is very difficult It makes you believe that it is cleaning seriously. As for the supporting facilities, I only went to the gym and swimming pool. It should not be called a gym but an activity room. There are few and incomplete equipment. The depth of the swimming pool is not 1.8, and it is still a steel structure. It is relatively shallow. I don‚Äôt plan to swim after taking a look. I can only say that it is very coping. It is just for the five-star rating. I didn‚Äôt experience other supporting facilities. The configuration of three stars is five-star price. I have been to five-star hotels in too many places, so there is a comparison. The difference is not a little bit, but the price is not bad. When I left, because the hotel parking lot is on B1, my car was parked in the negative one, and I had to pay 80 yuan for parking. The front desk was very indifferent to me and said that they could not coordinate for me. Only the area marked by the property was free. This is the first time I encountered such a situation. Haha, it is really awesome.
I also want to explain that the male staff at the front desk who checked me in met me 3 times in the elevator and lobby. I saw each other eye to eye, but did not say hello or nod, and just turned my head and left. It was so funny.
In conclusion, I can only say that this hotel has no management and no details. The staff does not even have basic courtesy. If a five-star hotel does not compete in service and details, what else can it compete in? The leadership has changed.
